## Mission

Verify the Issue is already resolved at HEAD and ship a verification artifact.

## Verification (HONEST)

The breakdown's binding requirements are:
1. Fix `_default_llm_completion` to drive async `OpenRouterClient.generate` via `asyncio.run`.
2. Raise RuntimeError if called from running event loop.
3. Smoke test under real key returns `scope_class=clinical_efficacy`.
4. 5 regression tests.

**Verification at HEAD (polaris branch, post-I-f2-008 merge):**

- **Fix #1 + #2 are in place at `src/polaris_graph/scope/clinical_classifier.py:214-243`.** The function:
  - Lazy-imports `asyncio` + `OpenRouterClient`.
  - Calls `asyncio.get_running_loop()` to detect existing loop.
  - Raises `RuntimeError("_default_llm_completion called from an async context; ...")` when a loop is running.
  - On the no-loop branch, calls `asyncio.run(client.generate(prompt=prompt, temperature=0.0, max_tokens=200))`.
  - Returns `result.content if hasattr(result, "content") else str(result)`.

- **Fix #4: 5 regression tests exist and PASS.** `tests/polaris_graph/scope/test_default_llm_completion_async_fix.py` contains:
  1. `test_default_llm_completion_awaits_async_generate`
  2. `test_default_llm_completion_inside_running_loop_raises`
  3. `test_llm_fallback_classify_returns_efficacy_when_llm_works`
  4. `test_llm_fallback_returns_uncertain_when_client_construction_fails`
  5. `test_default_llm_completion_passes_kwargs_to_generate`

  All 5 pass: `PYTHONPATH=src python -m pytest tests/polaris_graph/scope/test_default_llm_completion_async_fix.py -v` → `5 passed in 4.14s`. (PYTHONPATH=src required because the project does not pip-install itself; per Codex iter-1 P1 #2.)

- **Fix #3 (smoke test under real key):** Requires `OPENROUTER_API_KEY` and a network call. NOT executed autonomously per §8.4 resource discipline + cost concerns. The unit-level evidence (test #3 above) covers the same behavior with a stub `completion_fn`. User is welcome to run a one-shot real-key smoke any time; this Issue does not block on it.

## Risks for Codex Red-Team

1. **Empty canonical diff.** SHA stamps the empty patch. Codex reviews this brief + the verification doc to confirm the bug IS already fixed at the cited file:line refs.

2. **Verification reproducibility.** Codex can re-run `pytest tests/polaris_graph/scope/test_default_llm_completion_async_fix.py -v` independently to confirm 5/5 pass.

3. **Smoke test under real key.** Per §8.4 + cost: NOT executed in this Issue. Test #3 (`test_llm_fallback_classify_returns_efficacy_when_llm_works`) covers the same behavior with a stubbed `completion_fn` returning a canned `clinical_efficacy` JSON response. Acceptable substitute for unit-level verification.

4. **`asyncio.get_running_loop()` behavior.** Returns the loop if one is running, raises RuntimeError otherwise. Test #2 asserts the expected RuntimeError when called inside `asyncio.run()`.

5. **`asyncio.run()` semantics.** Creates a new loop, runs the coroutine, closes the loop. Cannot be called from inside a running loop (Python raises). The guard at lines 228-237 surfaces the misuse before `asyncio.run()` would itself raise.

6. **`hasattr(result, "content")` defensive.** OpenRouterClient.generate returns an `LLMResponse` with a `.content` attr. The `else str(result)` fallback handles edge cases where `generate` is mocked to return a plain string (test #1 + #5).

7. **No new package.json / requirements.txt dep.**

8. **CHARTER §1 LOC cap.** 0 source-code LOC; cap inapplicable.

 214: def _default_llm_completion(prompt: str) -> str:
 215:     """Production LLM call — lazy import + low-temp small model.
 216: 
 217:     OpenRouterClient.generate is async; this sync helper runs it via
 218:     asyncio.run. If we are already inside a running event loop (e.g. an
 219:     async test or async FastAPI handler) we raise RuntimeError so the
 220:     caller surfaces the misuse instead of silently returning "uncertain"
 221:     via the outer try/except in llm_fallback_classify (LAW II — no
 222:     silent fallback).
 223:     """
 224:     import asyncio
 225: 
 226:     from polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import OpenRouterClient
 227: 
 228:     try:
 229:         asyncio.get_running_loop()
 230:     except RuntimeError:
 231:         pass  # No running loop — safe to use asyncio.run
 232:     else:
 233:         raise RuntimeError(
 234:             "_default_llm_completion called from an async context; "
 235:             "callers in async code must invoke OpenRouterClient.generate "
 236:             "directly with await, not through this sync wrapper."
 237:         )
 238: 
 239:     client = OpenRouterClient()
 240:     result = asyncio.run(
 241:         client.generate(prompt=prompt, temperature=0.0, max_tokens=200)
 242:     )
 243:     return result.content if hasattr(result, "content") else str(result)
 244: 
 245: 
 246: _VALID_LLM_CLASSES = {
 247:     "clinical_efficacy",
 248:     "clinical_safety",
 249:     "clinical_diagnosis",
 250:     "clinical_prognosis",
 251:     "out_of_scope",
 252: }
 253: 
 254: 
 255: def _parse_llm_response(raw: str) -> tuple[str, float]:
 256:     """Extract value + confidence from LLM JSON response.
 257: 
 258:     Robust to: leading/trailing whitespace, markdown code fences, prose
 259:     wrappers. Returns ('uncertain', 0.0) if parsing fails entirely.
 260:     """
 261:     if not raw:
 262:         return ("uncertain", 0.0)
 263:     # Strip common markdown wrappers
 264:     text = raw.strip()
 265:     if text.startswith("```"):
 266:         # Find the first { and last }
 267:         start = text.find("{")
 268:         end = text.rfind("}")
 269:         if start != -1 and end != -1:
 270:             text = text[start:end + 1]
 271:     try:
 272:         parsed = json.loads(text)
 273:     except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
 274:         # Last-ditch: try to find any {...} substring
 275:         match = re.search(r"\{[^{}]*\}", text, re.DOTALL)
 276:         if not match:
 277:             return ("uncertain", 0.0)
 278:         try:
 279:             parsed = json.loads(match.group(0))
 280:         except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError):
 281:             return ("uncertain", 0.0)
 282:     if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
 283:         return ("uncertain", 0.0)
 284:     value = str(parsed.get("value", "")).strip()
 285:     if value not in _VALID_LLM_CLASSES:
 286:         return ("uncertain", 0.0)
 287:     try:
 288:         confidence = float(parsed.get("confidence", 0.5))
 289:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
 290:         confidence = 0.5
 291:     confidence = max(0.0, min(1.0, confidence))
 292:     return (value, confidence)
 293: 
 294: 
 295: def llm_fallback_classify(
 296:     normalized_text: str,
 297:     *,
 298:     completion_fn: Callable[[str], str] | None = None,
 299: ) -> ScopeClass:
 300:     """Second-layer LLM classification for questions where regex returned uncertain.
 301: 
 302:     Args:
 303:         normalized_text: question text post-normalization
 304:         completion_fn: dependency-injectable LLM caller. Defaults to
 305:                        _default_llm_completion (real OpenRouter call).
 306:                        Tests pass mocks.
 307: 
 308:     Returns:
 309:         ScopeClass with provenance="llm_fallback" and the LLM-derived value.
 310:         Falls back to ScopeClass(value="uncertain", confidence=0.0) on ANY
 311:         failure (no API key, network error, malformed response, etc.) so
 312:         the pipeline degrades gracefully.
 313:     """
 314:     if not isinstance(normalized_text, str):
 315:         raise TypeError(
 316:             f"llm_fallback_classify expected str, got {type(normalized_text).__name__}"
 317:         )
 318: 
 319:     fn = completion_fn or _default_llm_completion
 320:     prompt = LLM_PROMPT_TEMPLATE.format(question=normalized_text)
 321: 
 322:     try:
 323:         raw_response = fn(prompt)
 324:     except Exception:
 325:         # Graceful degradation — LLM unavailable, missing key, network error, etc.
 326:         return ScopeClass(
 327:             value="uncertain",
 328:             confidence=0.0,
 329:             provenance="llm_fallback",
 330:             matched_pattern=None,

  22: 
  23: The bug fix at `src/polaris_graph/scope/clinical_classifier.py:214-243` correctly:
  24: 1. Detects a running event loop via `asyncio.get_running_loop()` (lines 228-237).
  25: 2. Raises RuntimeError when called from async context (lines 232-237).
  26: 3. Drives `OpenRouterClient.generate` via `asyncio.run` on the no-loop branch (lines 239-242).
  27: 4. Returns `result.content` (or `str(result)` fallback) (line 243).
  28: 
  29: The 5 regression tests in `tests/polaris_graph/scope/test_default_llm_completion_async_fix.py` cover:
  30: 1. Async generate is awaited (mock returning canned LLMResponse).
  31: 2. RuntimeError raises inside `asyncio.run()`.
  32: 3. End-to-end `llm_fallback_classify` returns `clinical_efficacy` with stub.
  33: 4. Returns `uncertain` on client construction failure (no API key).
  34: 5. kwargs (`temperature`, `max_tokens`) passed through to `generate`.
  35: 
  36: ## Verdict
  37: 
  38: APPROVE for Codex diff review.

   1: """Regression test for the async/sync collision in clinical_classifier.
   2: 
   3: Bug: `_default_llm_completion` called `OpenRouterClient.generate()` (which
   4: is async) without awaiting it. The returned coroutine was passed to
   5: `_parse_llm_response`, which couldn't parse it, returning ('uncertain',
   6: 0.0). The outer try/except in `llm_fallback_classify` then masked the
   7: RuntimeWarning. Net effect: every LLM-fallback classification silently
   8: returned 'uncertain' under real keys, breaking the Sep 6 demo flow.
   9: 
  10: This test pins the contract: when the async client is mocked to return a
  11: proper LLMResponse-shaped object, _default_llm_completion must invoke it
  12: correctly and return the .content string.
  13: """

  54:     """The async generate() must be awaited; the return must be its .content."""

state\polaris_restart\issue_github_map.json:9:  "I-bug-079": 106,
state\polaris_restart\plan.md:343:- **I-BUG-079** — Async/sync collision in `clinical_classifier._default_llm_completion`. The function calls `OpenRouterClient.generate()` (async) as if sync, returning a coroutine that fails downstream and silently classifies the canonical demo question as `out_of_scope` under real keys. Fix: `asyncio.run(client.generate(...))` + `RuntimeError` if called from inside an event loop. Acceptance: smoke test `process_intake("Is high-dose aspirin effective for migraine in adults?")` returns `scope_class=clinical_efficacy` under real key. Triage: scheduled into Phase 1 sequence after I-F1-001 (scope discovery substrate revival).
state\polaris_restart\plan.md:493:- "The bugs come back" is not a cost — it's the proof that the gates work. If Codex audits the un-fixed code and does NOT flag the async/sync collision, the gates failed and we learn that. If Codex DOES flag it, the gates worked.
state\polaris_restart\plan_amendment_skip_road_b_reset.md:68:4. **Could a bug in PR #79 / #82 / #84 fixes be hidden by accepting them as live?** The bugs were real (async/sync collision, etc.). The fixes are in the code. Under the amendment, I-BUG-* Issues become re-audit-not-re-fix work. If Codex audit finds the live fix is wrong, a follow-up PR fixes it. No worse than re-fixing under strict §7.D.

.codex\pr_b_dna_doc_updates_review_verdict_iter_7.txt:6459:+- **I-BUG-079** — Async/sync collision in `clinical_classifier._default_llm_completion`. The function calls `OpenRouterClient.generate()` (async) as if sync, returning a coroutine that fails downstream and silently classifies the canonical demo question as `out_of_scope` under real keys. Fix: `asyncio.run(client.generate(...))` + `RuntimeError` if called from inside an event loop. Acceptance: smoke test `process_intake("Is high-dose aspirin effective for migraine in adults?")` returns `scope_class=clinical_efficacy` under real key. Triage: scheduled into Phase 1 sequence after I-F1-001 (scope discovery substrate revival).

.codex\pr_d_mechanical_gates_review_verdict_iter_5.txt:86:- **PRD3-P2-002 FIXED — issue-id regex tightened to canonical schema.** Replaced `^bot/([A-Za-z0-9_-]+)$` (loose alphabet) with `^bot/(I-[a-z0-9]{2,8}-[0-9]{3}(-[a-z0-9_-]+)?)$` (matches issue_breakdown.md §3 schema). .codex\pr_b_dna_doc_updates_review_verdict_iter_8.txt:2131:+- **I-BUG-079** — Async/sync collision in `clinical_classifier._default_llm_completion`. The function calls `OpenRouterClient.generate()` (async) as if sync, returning a coroutine that fails downstream and silently classifies the canonical demo question as `out_of_scope` under real keys. Fix: `asyncio.run(client.generate(...))` + `RuntimeError` if called from inside an event loop. Acceptance: smoke test `process_intake("Is high-dose aspirin effective for migraine in adults?")` returns `scope_class=clinical_efficacy` under real key. Triage: scheduled into Phase 1 sequence after I-F1-001 (scope discovery substrate revival).
